\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__brick__element_8cc_source_l01266}01266 \textcolor{comment}{  /// Build the element by doing the following:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__brick__element_8cc_source_l01267}01267 \textcolor{comment}{  /// -\/ Give it nodal positions (by establishing the pointers to its}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__brick__element_8cc_source_l01269}01269 \textcolor{comment}{  /// -\/ In the process create new nodes where required (i.e. if they}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__brick__element_8cc_source_l01270}01270 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   don't exist in father element or have already been created}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__brick__element_8cc_source_l01271}01271 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   while building new neighbour elements). Node building}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__brick__element_8cc_source_l01272}01272 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   involves the following steps:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__brick__element_8cc_source_l01273}01273 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   -\/ Get nodal position from father element.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__brick__element_8cc_source_l01274}01274 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   -\/ Establish the time-\/history of the newly created nodal point}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__brick__element_8cc_source_l01275}01275 \textcolor{comment}{  ///     (its coordinates and the previous values) consistent with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__brick__element_8cc_source_l01276}01276 \textcolor{comment}{  ///     the father's history.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__brick__element_8cc_source_l01277}01277 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   -\/ Determine the boundary conditions of the nodes (newly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__brick__element_8cc_source_l01278}01278 \textcolor{comment}{  ///     created nodes can only lie on the interior of any}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__brick__element_8cc_source_l01279}01279 \textcolor{comment}{  ///     edges of the father element -\/-\/ this makes it possible to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__brick__element_8cc_source_l01280}01280 \textcolor{comment}{  ///     to figure out what their bc should be...)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__brick__element_8cc_source_l01281}01281 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   -\/ Add node to the mesh's stoarge scheme for the boundary nodes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__brick__element_8cc_source_l01282}01282 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   -\/ Add the new node to the mesh itself}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__brick__element_8cc_source_l01283}01283 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   -\/ Doc newly created nodes in file "{}new\_nodes.dat"{} in the directory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__brick__element_8cc_source_l01284}01284 \textcolor{comment}{  /// /    of the DocInfo object (only if it's open!)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__brick__element_8cc_source_l01285}01285 \textcolor{comment}{  /// -\/ Finally, excute the element-\/specific further\_build()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__brick__element_8cc_source_l01286}01286 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   (empty by default -\/-\/ must be overloaded for specific elements).}}
